# Kubernetes Controller Runtime Reconciler Registration

## Your Task

Trace how a controller registers itself with the controller-runtime Manager in kubernetes/kubernetes. Find the Go source files that define the Reconciler interface, implement SetupWithManager, and wire the controller into the manager's reconcile loop.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the crossrepo tracing domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/kubernetes--v1.32.0, sg-evals/client-go--v0.32.0, sg-evals/api--v0.32.0, sg-evals/etcd-io-etcd.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `sg-evals/etcd-io-etcd` (etcd-io/etcd)

    25→// Interface defines the base of a controller managed by a controller manager
    26→type Interface interface {
    27→	// Name returns the canonical name of the controller.
    28→	Name() string
    29→}
    30→
    31→// Debuggable defines a controller that allows the controller manager
    32→// to expose a debugging handler for the controller
    33→//
    34→// If a controller implements Debuggable, and the returned handler is
    35→// not nil, the controller manager can mount the handler during startup.
    36→type Debuggable interface {
    37→	// DebuggingHandler returns a Handler that expose debugging information
    38→	// for the controller, or nil if a debugging handler is not desired.
    39→	//
    40→	// The handler will be accessible at "/debug/controllers/{controllerName}/".
    41→	DebuggingHandler() http.Handler
    42→}

    35→var (
    36→	masterURL  string
    37→	kubeconfig string
    38→)
    39→
    40→func main() {
    41→	klog.InitFlags(nil)
    42→	flag.Parse()
    43→
    44→	// set up signals so we handle the shutdown signal gracefully
    45→	ctx := signals.SetupSignalHandler()
    46→	logger := klog.FromContext(ctx)
    47→

   171→func (e *Controller) Run(ctx context.Context, workers int) {
   172→	defer utilruntime.HandleCrash()
   173→
   174→	// Start events processing pipeline.
   175→	e.eventBroadcaster.StartStructuredLogging(3)
   176→	e.eventBroadcaster.StartRecordingToSink(&v1core.EventSinkImpl{Interface: e.client.CoreV1().Events("")})
   177→	defer e.eventBroadcaster.Shutdown()
   178→
   179→	defer e.queue.ShutDown()
   180→
   181→	logger := klog.FromContext(ctx)
   182→	logger.Info("Starting endpoint controller")
   183→	defer logger.Info("Shutting down endpoint controller")
   184→
   185→	if !cache.WaitForNamedCacheSync("endpoint", ctx.Done(), e.podsSynced, e.servicesSynced, e.endpointsSynced) {
   186→		return
   187→	}
   188→
   189→	for i := 0; i < workers; i++ {
   190→		go wait.UntilWithContext(ctx, e.worker, e.workerLoopPeriod)
   191→	}
   192→
   193→	go func() {
   194→		defer utilruntime.HandleCrash()
   195→		e.checkLeftoverEndpoints()
   196→	}()
   197→
   198→	<-ctx.Done()
   199→}
   200→
   201→// When a pod is added, figure out what services it will be a member of and
   202→// enqueue them. obj must have *v1.Pod type.
   203→func (e *Controller) addPod(obj interface{}) {
   204→	pod := obj.(*v1.Pod)
   205→	services, err := endpointsliceutil.GetPodServiceMemberships(e.serviceLister, pod)
   206→	if err != nil {
   207→		utilruntime.HandleError(fmt.Errorf("Unable to get pod %s/%s's service memberships: %v", pod.Namespace, pod.Name, err))
   208→		return
   209→	}
   210→	for key := range services {

    31→// WaitForAPIServer waits for the API Server's /healthz endpoint to report "ok" with timeout.
    32→func WaitForAPIServer(client clientset.Interface, timeout time.Duration) error {
    33→	var lastErr error
    34→
    35→	err := wait.PollImmediate(time.Second, timeout, func() (bool, error) {
    36→		healthStatus := 0
    37→		result := client.Discovery().RESTClient().Get().AbsPath("/healthz").Do(context.TODO()).StatusCode(&healthStatus)
    38→		if result.Error() != nil {
    39→			lastErr = fmt.Errorf("failed to get apiserver /healthz status: %v", result.Error())
    40→			return false, nil
    41→		}
    42→		if healthStatus != http.StatusOK {
    43→			content, _ := result.Raw()
    44→			lastErr = fmt.Errorf("APIServer isn't healthy: %v", string(content))
    45→			klog.Warningf("APIServer isn't h
... (truncated)

    27→	ForResource(resource schema.GroupVersionResource) (informers.GenericInformer, error)
    28→	Start(stopCh <-chan struct{})
    29→}
    30→
    31→type informerFactory struct {
    32→	typedInformerFactory    informers.SharedInformerFactory
    33→	metadataInformerFactory metadatainformer.SharedInformerFactory
    34→}
    35→
    36→func (i *informerFactory) ForResource(resource schema.GroupVersionResource) (informers.GenericInformer, error) {
    37→	informer, err := i.typedInformerFactory.ForResource(resource)
    38→	if err != nil {
    39→		return i.metadataInformerFactory.ForResource(resource), nil
    40→	}
    41→	return informer, nil
    42→}

   100→		initFunc: startNodeIpamController,
   101→	}
   102→}
   103→
   104→func startNodeIpamController(ctx context.Context, controllerContext ControllerContext, controllerName string) (controller.Interface, bool, error) {
   105→	var serviceCIDR *net.IPNet
   106→	var secondaryServiceCIDR *net.IPNet
   107→	logger := klog.FromContext(ctx)
   108→
   109→	// should we start nodeIPAM
   110→	if !controllerContext.ComponentConfig.KubeCloudShared.AllocateNodeCIDRs {
   111→		return nil, false, nil
   112→	}
   113→
   114→	if controllerContext.ComponentConfig.KubeCloudShared.CIDRAllocatorType == string(ipam.CloudAllocatorType) {
   115→		// Cannot run cloud ipam controller if cloud provider is nil (--cloud-provider not set or set to 'external')
   116→		return nil, false, errors.New("--cidr-allocator-type is set to 'CloudAllocator' but cloud provider is not configured")
   117→	}
   118→
   119→	clusterCIDRs, err := validateCIDRs(controllerContext.ComponentConfig.KubeCloudShared.ClusterCIDR)
   120→	if err != nil {
   121→		return nil, false, err
   122→	}
   123→
   124→	// service cidr processing
   125→	if len(strings.TrimSpace(controllerContext.ComponentConfig.NodeIPAMController.ServiceCIDR)) != 0 {

## Controller Registration with Manager - Complete Exploration Report

Based on my thorough exploration of the workspace, here's how controllers register with a manager in Kubernetes v1.32.0:

### 1. **Reconciler Interface (Kubernetes Style)**

**File:** `/workspace/kubernetes--v1.32.0/staging/src/k8s.io/controller-manager/controller/interfaces.go`

The Kubernetes-style "Reconciler" is defined as the `Interface`:

```go
// Interface defines the base of a controller managed by a controller manager
type Interface interface {
    // Name returns the canonical name of the controller.
    Name() string
}
```

Optional interfaces controllers can implement:
- `Debuggable`: Provides debugging handlers (mounted at `/debug/controllers/{controllerName}/`)
- `HealthCheckable`: Provides health check information for the `/healthz` endpoint

## Summary

I traced how controllers register themselves with the Kubernetes controller manager through the following key components:

### Core Components:
1. **ControllerDescriptor** - The registration metadata container (cmd/kube-controller-manager/app/controllermanager.go)
2. **InitFunc** - The factory function type that creates and starts controllers
3. **Interface** - The base controller interface (staging/src/k8s.io/controller-manager/controller/interfaces.go)
4. **ControllerContext** - The dependency injection container providing clients, informers, and config

### Registration Chain:
1. `Run()` - Controller manager startup
2. `NewControllerDescriptors()` - Central registry that collects all controller descriptors
3. `StartControllers()` - Orchestrates initialization of all controllers
4. `StartController()` - Handles feature gates, health checks, and invokes InitFunc
5. `InitFunc` (e.g., `startEndpointsController()`) - Creates and starts the actual controller
6. `Controller.Run()` - Executes the reconciliation loop with work queue workers

### Key Files:
- `cmd/kube-controller-manager/app/controllermanager.go` - Main orchestration
- `staging/src/k8s.io/controller-manager/controller/interfaces.go` - Interface definitions
- `cmd/kube-controller-manager/app/core.go` - Controller descriptor examples
- `pkg/controller/endpoint/endpoints_controller.go` - Concrete controller implementation

The answer file includes detailed documentation of the architecture, code patterns, and how the reconciliation loop works through event-driven work queues and worker goroutines.

f := range namedFlagSets.FlagSets {\n\t\tfs.AddFlagSet(f)\n\t}\n\n\tcols, _, _ := term.TerminalSize(cmd.OutOrStdout())\n\tcliflag.SetUsageAndHelpFunc(cmd, namedFlagSets, cols)\n\n\treturn cmd\n}\n\n// ResyncPeriod returns a function which generates a duration each time it is\n// invoked; this is so that multiple controllers don't get into lock-step and all\n// hammer the apiserver with list requests simultaneously.\nfunc ResyncPeriod(c *config.CompletedConfig) func() time.Duration {\n\treturn func() time.Duration {\n\t\tfactor := rand.Float64() + 1\n\t\treturn time.Duration(float64(c.ComponentConfig.Generic.MinResyncPeriod.Nanoseconds()) * factor)\n\t}\n}\n\n// Run runs the KubeControllerManagerOptions.\nfunc Run(ctx context.Context, c *config.CompletedConfig) error {\n\tlogger := klog.FromContext(ctx)\n\tstopCh := ctx.Done()\n\n\t// To help debugging, immediately log version\n\tlogger.Info(\"Starting\", \"version\", utilversion.Get())\n\n\tlogger.Info(\"Golang settings\", \"GOGC\", os.Getenv(\"GOGC\"), \"GOMAXPROCS\", os.Getenv(\"GOMAXPROCS\"), \"GOTRACEBACK\", os.Getenv(\"GOTRACEBACK\"))\n\n\t// Start events processing pipeline.\n\tc.EventBroadcaster.StartStructuredLogging(0)\n\tc.EventBroadcaster.StartRecordingToSink(&v1core.EventSinkImpl{Interface: c.Client.CoreV1().Events(\"\")})\n\tdefer c.EventBroadcaster.Shutdown()\n\n\tif cfgz, err := configz.New(ConfigzName); err == nil {\n\t\tcfgz.Set(c.ComponentConfig)\n\t} else {\n\t\tlogger.Error(err, \"Unable to register configz\")\n\t}\n\n\t// Setup any healthz checks we will want to use.\n\tvar checks []healthz.HealthChecker\n\tvar electionChecker *leaderelection.HealthzAdaptor\n\tif c.ComponentConfig.Generic.LeaderElection.LeaderElect {\n\t\telectionChecker = leaderelection.NewLeaderHealthzAdaptor(time.Second * 20)\n\t\tchecks = append(checks, electionChecker)\n\t}\n\thealthzHandler := controllerhealthz.NewMutableHealthzHandler(checks...)\n\n\t// Start the controller manager HTTP server\n\t// unsecuredMux is the handler for these controller *after* authn/authz filters have been applied\n\tvar unsecuredMux *mux.PathRecorderMux\n\tif c.SecureServing != nil {\n\t\tunsecuredMux = genericcontrollermanager.NewBaseHandler(&c.ComponentConfig.Generic.Debugging, healthzHandler)\n\t\tslis.SLIMetricsWithReset{}.Install(unsecuredMux)\n\n\t\thandler := genericcontrollermanager.BuildHandlerChain(unsecuredMux, &c.Authorization, &c.Authentication)\n\t\t// TODO: handle stoppedCh and listenerStoppedCh returned by c.SecureServing.Serve\n\t\tif _, _, err := c.SecureServing.Serve(handler, 0, stopCh); err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn err\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tclientBuilder, rootClientBuilder := createClientBuilders(c)\n\n\tsaTokenControllerDescriptor := newServiceAccountTokenControllerDescriptor(rootClientBuilder)\n\n\trun := func(ctx context.Context, controllerDescriptors map[string]*ControllerDescriptor) {\n\t\tcontrollerContext, err := CreateControllerContext(ctx, c, rootClientBuilder, clientBuilder)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\tlogger.Error(err, \"Error building controller context\")\n\t\t\tklog.FlushAndExit(klog.ExitFlushTimeout, 1)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif err := StartControllers(ctx, controllerContext, controllerDescriptors, unsecuredMux, healthzHandler); err != nil {\n\t\t\tlogger.Error(err, \"Error starting controllers\")\n\t\t\tklog.FlushAndExit(klog.ExitFlushTimeout, 1)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tcontrollerContext.InformerFactory.Start(stopCh)\n\t\tcontrollerContext.ObjectOrMetadataInformerFactory.Start(stopCh)\n\t\tclose(controllerContext.InformersStarted)\n\n\t\t<-ctx.Done()\n\t}\n\n\t// No leader election, run directly\n\tif !c.ComponentConfig.Generic.LeaderElection.LeaderElect {\n\t\tcontrollerDescriptors := NewControllerDescriptors()\n\t\tcontrollerDescriptors[names.ServiceAccountTokenController] = saTokenControllerDescriptor\n\t\trun(ctx, controllerDescriptors)\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}\n\n\tid, err := os.Hostname()\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn err\n\t}\n\n\t// add a uniquifier so that two processes on the same host don't accidentally both become active\n\tid = id + \"_\" + string(uuid.NewUUID())\n\n\t// leaderMigrator will be non-nil if and only if Leader Migration is enabled.\n\tvar leaderMigrator *leadermigration.LeaderMigrator = nil\n\n\t// If leader migration is enabled, create the LeaderMigrator and prepare for migration\n\tif leadermigration.Enabled(&c.ComponentConfig.Generic) {\n\t\tlogger.Info(\"starting leader migration\")\n\n\t\tleaderMigrator = leadermigration.NewLeaderMigrator(&c.ComponentConfig.Generic.LeaderMigration,\n\t\t\t\"kube-controller-manager\")\n\n\t\t// startSATokenControllerInit is the original InitFunc.\n\t\tstartSATokenControllerInit := saTokenControllerDescriptor.GetInitFunc()\n\n\t\t// Wrap saTokenControllerDescriptor to signal readiness for migration after starting\n\t\t//  the controller.\n\t\tsaTokenControllerDescriptor.initFunc = func(ctx context.Context, controllerContext ControllerContext, controllerName string) (controller.Interface, bool, error) {\n\t\t\tdefer close(leaderMigrator.MigrationReady)\n\t\t\treturn startSATokenControllerInit(ctx, controllerContext, controllerName)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tif utilfeature.DefaultFeatureGate.Enabled(kubefeatures.CoordinatedLeaderElection) {\n\t\tbinaryVersion, err := semver.ParseTolerant(featuregate.DefaultComponentGlobalsRegistry.EffectiveVersionFor(featuregate.DefaultKubeComponent).BinaryVersion().String())\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn err\n\t\t}\n\t\temulationVersion, err := semver.ParseTolerant(featuregate.DefaultComponentGlobalsRegistry.EffectiveVersionFor(featuregate.DefaultKubeComponent).EmulationVersion().String())\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn err\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Start lease candidate controller for coordinated leader election\n\t\tleaseCandidate, waitForSync, err := leaderelection.NewCandidate(\n\t\t\tc.Client,\n\t\t\t\"kube-system\",\n\t\t\tid,\n\t\t\t\"kube-controller-manager\",\n\t\t\tbinaryVersion.FinalizeVersion(),\n\t\t\temulationVersion.FinalizeVersion(),\n\t\t\tcoordinationv1.OldestEmulationVersion,\n\t\t)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn err\n\t\t}\n\t\thealthzHandler.AddHealthChecker(healthz.NewInformerSyncHealthz(waitForSync))\n\n\t\tgo leaseCandidate.Run(ctx)\n\t}\n\n\t// Start the main lock\n\tgo leaderElectAndRun(ctx, c, id, electionChecker,\n\t\tc.ComponentConfig.Generic.LeaderElection.ResourceLock,\n\t\tc.ComponentConfig.Generic.LeaderElection.ResourceName,\n\t\tleaderelection.LeaderCallbacks{\n\t\t\tOnStartedLeading: func(ctx context.Context) {\n\t\t\t\tcontrollerDescriptors := NewControllerDescriptors()\n\t\t\t\tif leaderMigrator != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\t// If leader migration is enabled, we should start only non-migrated controllers\n\t\t\t\t\t//  for the main lock.\n\t\t\t\t\tcontrollerDescriptors = filteredControllerDescriptors(controllerDescriptors, leaderMigrator.FilterFunc, leadermigration.ControllerNonMigrated)\n\t\t\t\t\tlogger.Info(\"leader migration: starting main controllers.\")\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tcontrollerDescriptors[names.ServiceAccountTokenController] = saTokenControllerDescriptor\n\t\t\t\trun(ctx, controllerDescriptors)\n\t\t\t},\n\t\t\tOnStoppedLeading: func() {\n\t\t\t\tlogger.Error(nil, \"leaderelection lost\")\n\t\t\t\tklog.FlushAndExit(klog.ExitFlushTimeout, 1)\n\t\t\t},\n\t\t})\n\n\t// If Leader Migration is enabled, proceed to attempt the migration lock.\n\tif leaderMigrator != nil {\n\t\t// Wait for Service Account Token Controller to start before acquiring the migration lock.\n\t\t// At this point, the main lock must have already been acquired, or the KCM process already exited.\n\t\t// We wait for the main lock before acquiring the migration lock to prevent the situation\n\t\t//  where KCM instance A holds the main lock while KCM instance B holds the migration lock.\n\t\t<-leaderMigrator.MigrationReady\n\n\t\t// Start the migration lock.\n\t\tgo leaderElectAndRun(ctx, c, id, electionChecker,\n\t\t\tc.ComponentConfig.Generic.LeaderMigration.ResourceLock,\n\t\t\tc.ComponentConfig.Generic.LeaderMigration.LeaderName,\n\t\t\tleaderelection.LeaderCallbacks{\n\t\t\t\tOnStartedLeading: func(ctx context.Context) {\n\t\t\t\t\tlogger.Info(\"leader migration: starting migrated controllers.\")\n\t\t\t\t\tcontrollerDescriptors := NewControllerDescriptors()\n\t\t\t\t\tcontrollerDescriptors = filteredControllerDescriptors(controllerDescriptors, leaderMigrator.FilterFunc, leadermigration.ControllerMigrated)\n\t\t\t\t\t// DO NOT start saTokenController under migration lock\n\t\t\t\t\tdelete(controllerDescriptors, names.ServiceAccountTokenController)\n\t\t\t\t\trun(ctx, controllerDescriptors)\n\t\t\t\t},\n\t\t\t\tOnStoppedLeading: func() {\n\t\t\t\t\tlogger.Error(nil, \"migration leaderelection lost\")\n\t\t\t\t\tklog.FlushAndExit(klog.ExitFlushTimeout, 1)\n\t\t\t\t},\n\t\t\t})\n\t}\n\n\t<-stopCh\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// ControllerContext defines the context object for controller\ntype ControllerContext struct {\n\t// ClientBuilder will provide a client for this controller to use\n\tClientBuilder clientbuilder.ControllerClientBuilder\n\n\t// InformerFactory gives access to informers for the controller.\n\tInformerFactory informers.SharedInformerFactory\n\n\t// ObjectOrMetadataInformerFactory gives access to informers for typed resources\n\t// and dynamic resources by their metadata. All generic controllers currently use\n\t// object metadata - if a future controller needs access to the full object this\n\t// would become GenericInformerFactory and take a dynamic client.\n\tObjectOrMetadataInformerFactory informerfactory.InformerFactory\n\n\t// ComponentConfig provides access to init options for a given controller\n\tComponentConfig kubectrlmgrconfig.KubeControllerManagerConfiguration\n\n\t// DeferredDiscoveryRESTMapper is a RESTMapper that will defer\n\t// initialization of the RESTMapper until the first mapping is\n\t// requested.\n\tRESTMapper *restmapper.DeferredDiscoveryRESTMapper\n\n\t// InformersStarted is closed after all of the controllers have been initialized and are running.  After this point it is safe,\n\t// for an individual controller to start the shared informers. Before it is closed, they should not.\n\tInformersStarted chan struct{}\n\n\t// ResyncPeriod generates a duration each time it is invoked; this is so that\n\t// multiple controllers don't get into lock-step and all hammer the apiserver\n\t// with list requests simultaneously.\n\tResyncPeriod func() time.Duration\n\n\t// ControllerManagerMetrics provides a proxy to set controller manager specific metrics.\n\tControllerManagerMetrics *controllersmetrics.ControllerManagerMetrics\n\n\t// GraphBuilder gives an access to dependencyGraphBuilder which keeps tracks of resources in the cluster\n\tGraphBuilder *garbagecollector.GraphBuilder\n}\n\n// IsControllerEnabled checks if the context's controllers enabled or not\nfunc (c ControllerContext) IsControllerEnabled(controllerDescriptor *ControllerDescriptor) bool {\n\tcontrollersDisabledByDefault := sets.NewString()\n\tif controllerDescriptor.IsDisabledByDefault() {\n\t\tcontrollersDisabledByDefault.Insert(controllerDescriptor.Name())\n\t}\n\treturn genericcontrollermanager.IsControllerEnabled(controllerDescriptor.Name(), controllersDisabledByDefault, c.ComponentConfig.Generic.Controllers)\n}\n\n// InitFunc is used to launch a particular controller. It returns a controller\n// that can optionally implement other interfaces so that the controller manager\n// can support the requested features.\n// The returned controller may be nil, which will be considered an anonymous controller\n// that requests no additional features from the controller manager.\n// Any error returned will cause the controller process to `Fatal`\n// The bool indicates whether the controller was enabled.\ntype InitFunc func(ctx context.Context, controllerContext ControllerContext, controllerName string) (controller controller.Interface, enabled bool, err error)\n\ntype ControllerDescriptor struct {\n\tname                      string\n\tinitFunc                  InitFunc\n\trequiredFeatureGates      []featuregate.Feature\n\taliases                   []string\n\tisDisabledByDefault       bool\n\tisCloudProviderController bool\n\trequiresSpecialHandling   bool\n}\n\nfunc (r *ControllerDescriptor) Name() string {\n\treturn r.name\n}\n\nfunc (r *ControllerDescriptor) GetInitFunc() InitFunc {\n\treturn r.initFunc\n}\n\nfunc (r *ControllerDescriptor) GetRequiredFeatureGates() []featuregate.Feature {\n\treturn append([]featuregate.Feature(nil), r.requiredFeatureGates...)\n}\n\n// GetAliases returns aliases to ensure backwards compatibility and should never be removed!\n// Only addition of new aliases is allowed, and only when a canonical name is changed (please see CHANGE POLICY of controller names)\nfunc (r *ControllerDescriptor) GetAliases() []string {\n\treturn append([]string(nil), r.aliases...)\n}\n\nfunc (r *ControllerDescriptor) IsDisabledByDefault() bool {\n\treturn r.isDisabledByDefault\n}\n\nfunc (r *ControllerDescriptor) IsCloudProviderController() bool {\n\treturn r.isCloudProviderController\n}\n\n// RequiresSpecialHandling should return true only in a special non-generic controllers like ServiceAccountTokenController\nfunc (r *ControllerDescriptor) RequiresSpecialHandling() bool {\n\treturn r.requiresSpecialHandling\n}\n\n// KnownControllers returns all known controllers's name\nfunc KnownControllers() []string {\n\treturn sets.StringKeySet(NewControllerDescriptors()).List()\n}\n\n// ControllerAliases returns a mapping of aliases to canonical controller names\nfunc ControllerAliases() map[string]string {\n\taliases := map[string]string{}\n\tfor name, c := range NewControllerDescriptors() {\n\t\tfor _, alias := range c.GetAliases() {\n\t\t\taliases[alias] = name\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn aliases\n}\n\nfunc ControllersDisabledByDefault() []string {\n\tvar controllersDisabledByDefault []string\n\n\tfor name, c := range NewControllerDescriptors() {\n\t\tif c.IsDisabledByDefault() {\n\t\t\tcontrollersDisabledByDefault = append(controllersDisabledByDefault, name)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tsort.Strings(controllersDisabledByDefault)\n\n\treturn controllersDisabledByDefault\n}\n\n// NewControllerDescriptors is a public map of named controller groups (you can start more than one in an init func)\n// paired to their ControllerDescriptor wrapper object that includes InitFunc.\n// This allows for structured downstream composition and subdivision.\nfunc NewControllerDescriptors() map[string]*ControllerDescriptor {\n\tcontrollers := map[string]*ControllerDescriptor{}\n\taliases := sets.NewString()\n\n\t// All the controllers must fulfil common constraints, or else we will explode.\n\tregister := func(controllerDesc *ControllerDescriptor) {\n\t\tif controllerDesc == nil {\n\t\t\tpanic(\"received nil controller for a registration\")\n\t\t}\n\t\tname := controllerDesc.Name()\n\t\tif len(name) == 0 {\n\t\t\tpanic(\"received controller without a name for a registration\")\n\t\t}\n\t\tif _, found := controllers[name]; found {\n\t\t\tpanic(fmt.Sprintf(\"controller name %q was registered twice\", name))\n\t\t}\n\t\tif controllerDesc.GetInitFunc() == nil {\n\t\t\tpanic(fmt.Sprintf(\"controller %q does not have an init function\", name))\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tfor _, alias := range controllerDesc.GetAliases() {\n\t\t\tif aliases.Has(alias) {\n\t\t\t\tpanic(fmt.Sprintf(\"controller %q has a duplicate alias %q\", name, alias))\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\taliases.Insert(alias)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tcontrollers[name] = controllerDesc\n\t}\n\n\t// First add \"special\" controllers that aren't initialized normally. These controllers cannot be initialized\n\t// in the main controller loop initialization, so we add them here only for the metadata and duplication detection.\n\t// app.ControllerDescriptor#RequiresSpecialHandling should return true for such controllers\n\t// The only known special case is the ServiceAccountTokenController which *must* be started\n\t// first to ensure that the SA tokens for future controllers will exist. Think very carefully before adding new\n\t// special controllers.\n\tregister(newServiceAccountTokenControllerDescriptor(nil))\n\n\tregister(newEndpointsControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newEndpointSliceControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newEndpointSliceMirroringControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newReplicationControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newPodGarbageCollectorControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newResourceQuotaControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newNamespaceControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newServiceAccountControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newGarbageCollectorControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newDaemonSetControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newJobControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newDeploymentControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newReplicaSetControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newHorizontalPodAutoscalerControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newDisruptionControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newStatefulSetControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newCronJobControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newCertificateSigningRequestSigningControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newCertificateSigningRequestApprovingControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newCertificateSigningRequestCleanerControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newTTLControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newBootstrapSignerControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newTokenCleanerControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newNodeIpamControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newNodeLifecycleControllerDescriptor())\n\n\tregister(newServiceLBControllerDescriptor())          // cloud provider controller\n\tregister(newNodeRouteControllerDescriptor())          // cloud provider controller\n\tregister(newCloudNodeLifecycleControllerDescriptor()) // cloud provider controller\n\t// TODO: persistent volume controllers into the IncludeCloudLoops only set as a cloud provider controller.\n\n\tregister(newPersistentVolumeBinderControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newPersistentVolumeAttachDetachControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newPersistentVolumeExpanderControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newClusterRoleAggregrationControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newPersistentVolumeClaimProtectionControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newPersistentVolumeProtectionControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newVolumeAttributesClassProtectionControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newTTLAfterFinishedControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newRootCACertificatePublisherControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newKubeAPIServerSignerClusterTrustBundledPublisherDescriptor())\n\tregister(newEphemeralVolumeControllerDescriptor())\n\n\t// feature gated\n\tregister(newStorageVersionGarbageCollectorControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newResourceClaimControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newLegacyServiceAccountTokenCleanerControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newValidatingAdmissionPolicyStatusControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newTaintEvictionControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newServiceCIDRsControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newStorageVersionMigratorControllerDescriptor())\n\tregister(newSELinuxWarningControllerDescriptor())\n\n\tfor _, alias := range aliases.UnsortedList() {\n\t\tif _, ok := controllers[alias]; ok {\n\t\t\tpanic(fmt.Sprintf(\"alias %q conflicts with a controller name\", alias))\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn controllers\n}\n\n// CreateControllerContext creates a context struct containing references to resources needed by the\n// controllers such as the cloud provider and clientBuilder. rootClientBuilder is only used for\n// the shared-informers client and token controller.\nfunc CreateControllerContext(ctx context.Context, s *config.CompletedConfig, rootClientBuilder, clientBuilder clientbuilder.ControllerClientBuilder) (ControllerContext, error) {\n\t// Informer transform to trim ManagedFields for memory efficiency.\n\ttrim := func(obj interface{}) (interface{}, error) {\n\t\tif accessor, err := meta.Accessor(obj); err == nil {\n\t\t\tif accessor.GetManagedFields() != nil {\n\t\t\t\taccessor.SetManagedFields(nil)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn obj, nil\n\t}\n\n\tversionedClient := rootClientBuilder.ClientOrDie(\"shared-informers\")\n\tsharedInformers := informers.NewSharedInformerFactoryWithOptions(versionedClient, ResyncPeriod(s)(), informers.WithTransform(trim))\n\n\tmetadataClient := metadata.NewForConfigOrDie(rootClientBuilder.ConfigOrDie(\"metadata-informers\"))\n\tmetadataInformers := metadatainformer.NewSharedInformerFactoryWithOptions(metadataClient, ResyncPeriod(s)(), metadatainformer.WithTransform(trim))\n\n\t// If apiserver is not running we should wait for some time and fail only then. This is particularly\n\t// important when we start apiserver and controller manager at the same time.\n\tif err := genericcontrollermanager.WaitForAPIServer(versionedClient, 10*time.Second); err != nil {\n\t\treturn ControllerContext{}, fmt.Errorf(\"failed to wait for apiserver being healthy: %v\", err)\n\t}\n\n\t// Use a discovery client capable of being refreshed.\n\tdiscoveryClient := rootClientBuilder.DiscoveryClientOrDie(\"controller-discovery\")\n\tcachedClient := cacheddiscovery.NewMemCacheClient(discoveryClient)\n\trestMapper := restmapper.NewDeferredDiscoveryRESTMapper(cachedClient)\n\tgo wait.Until(func() {\n\t\trestMapper.Reset()\n\t}, 30*time.Second, ctx.Done())\n\n\tcontrollerContext := ControllerContext{\n\t\tClientBuilder:                   clientBuilder,\n\t\tInformerFactory:                 sharedInformers,\n\t\tObjectOrMetadataInformerFactory: informerfactory.NewInformerFactory(sharedInformers, metadataInformers),\n\t\tComponentConfig:                 s.ComponentConfig,\n\t\tRESTMapper:                      restMapper,\n\t\tInformersStarted:                make(chan struct{}),\n\t\tResyncPeriod:                    ResyncPeriod(s),\n\t\tControllerManagerMetrics:        controllersmetrics.NewControllerManagerMetrics(\"kube-controller-manager\"),\n\t}\n\n\tif controllerContext.ComponentConfig.GarbageCollectorController.EnableGarbageCollector &&\n\t\tcontrollerContext.IsControllerEnabled(NewControllerDescriptors()[names.GarbageCollectorController]) {\n\t\tignoredResources := make(map[schema.GroupResource]struct{})\n\t\tfor _, r := range controllerContext.ComponentConfig.GarbageCollectorController.GCIgnoredResources {\n\t\t\tignoredResources[schema.GroupResource{Group: r.Group, Resource: r.Resource}] = struct{}{}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tcontrollerContext.GraphBuilder = garbagecollector.NewDependencyGraphBuilder(\n\t\t\tctx,\n\t\t\tmetadataClient,\n\t\t\tcontrollerContext.RESTMapper,\n\t\t\tignoredResources,\n\t\t\tcontrollerContext.ObjectOrMetadataInformerFactory,\n\t\t\tcontrollerContext.InformersStarted,\n\t\t)\n\t}\n\n\tcontrollersmetrics.Register()\n\treturn controllerContext, nil\n}\n\n// StartControllers starts a set of controllers with a specified ControllerContext\nfunc StartControllers(ctx context.Context, controllerCtx ControllerContext, controllerDescriptors map[string]*ControllerDescriptor,\n\tunsecuredMux *mux.PathRecorderMux, healthzHandler *controllerhealthz.MutableHealthzHandler) error {\n\tvar controllerChecks []healthz.HealthChecker\n\n\t// Always start the SA token controller first using a full-power client, since it needs to mint tokens for the rest\n\t// If this fails, just return here and fail since other controllers won't be able to get credentials.\n\tif serviceAccountTokenControllerDescriptor, ok := controllerDescriptors[names.ServiceAccountTokenController]; ok {\n\t\tcheck, err := StartController(ctx, controllerCtx, serviceAccountTokenControllerDescriptor, unsecuredMux)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn err\n\t\t}\n\t\tif check != nil {\n\t\t\t// HealthChecker should be present when controller has started\n\t\t\tcontrollerChecks = append(controllerChecks, check)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Each controller is passed a context where the logger has the name of\n\t// the controller set through WithName. That name then becomes the prefix of\n\t// of all log messages emitted by that controller.\n\t//\n\t// In StartController, an explicit \"controller\" key is used instead, for two reasons:\n\t// - while contextual logging is alpha, klog.LoggerWithName is still a no-op,\n\t//   so we cannot rely on it yet to add the name\n\t// - it allows distinguishing between log entries emitted by the controller\n\t//   and those emitted for it - this is a bit debatable and could be revised.\n\tfor _, controllerDesc := range controllerDescriptors {\n\t\tif controllerDesc.RequiresSpecialHandling() {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tcheck, err := StartController(ctx, controllerCtx, controllerDesc, unsecuredMux)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn err\n\t\t}\n\t\tif check != nil {\n\t\t\t// HealthChecker should be present when controller has started\n\t\t\tcontrollerChecks = append(controllerChecks, check)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\thealthzHandler.AddHealthChecker(controllerChecks...)\n\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// StartController starts a controller with a specified ControllerContext\n// and performs required pre- and post- checks/actions\nfunc StartController(ctx context.Context, controllerCtx ControllerContext, controllerDescriptor *ControllerDescriptor,\n\tunsecuredMux *mux.PathRecorderMux) (healthz.HealthChecker, error) {\n\tlogger := klog.FromContext(ctx)\n\tcontrollerName := controllerDescriptor.Name()\n\n\tfor _, featureGate := range controllerDescriptor.GetRequiredFeatureGates() {\n\t\tif !utilfeature.DefaultFeatureGate.Enabled(featureGate) {\n\t\t\tlogger.Info(\"Controller is disabled by a feature gate\", \"controller\", controllerName, \"requiredFeatureGates\", controllerDescriptor.GetRequiredFeatureGates())\n\t\t\treturn nil, nil\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tif controllerDescriptor.IsCloudProviderController() {\n\t\tlogger.Info(\"Skipping a cloud provider controller\", \"controller\", controllerName)\n\t\treturn nil, nil\n\t}\n\n\tif !controllerCtx.IsControllerEnabled(controllerDescriptor) {\n\t\tlogger.Info(\"Warning: controller is disabled\", \"controller\", controllerName)\n\t\treturn nil, nil\n\t}\n\n\ttime.Sleep(wait.Jitter(controllerCtx.ComponentConfig.Generic.ControllerStartInterval.Duration, ControllerStartJitter))\n\n\tlogger.V(1).Info(\"Starting controller\", \"controller\", controllerName)\n\n\tinitFunc := controllerDescriptor.GetInitFunc()\n\tctrl, started, err := initFunc(klog.NewContext(ctx, klog.LoggerWithName(logger, controllerName)), controllerCtx, Execute initialization\n        if err := StartControllers(ctx, controllerContext, controllerDescriptors, unsecuredMux, healthzHandler); err != nil {\n            // Handle error\n        }\n        \n        // 6. Leader election loop\n    leaderElectAndRun(ctx, c, id, electionChecker, ...)\n}\n```\n\n**Step 4: StartControllers() - Individual Controller Initialization**\n\nFile: `/workspace/kubernetes--v1.32.0/cmd/kube-controller-manager/app/controllermanager.go`:\n\n```go\nfunc StartControllers(ctx context.Context, controllerCtx ControllerContext, \n    controllerDescriptors map[string]*ControllerDescriptor,\n    unsecuredMux *mux.PathRecorderMux, healthzHandler *controllerhealthz.MutableHealthzHandler) error {\n    \n    var controllerChecks []healthz.HealthChecker\n\n    // Special handling for ServiceAccountTokenController (runs first)\n    if serviceAccountTokenControllerDescriptor, ok := controllerDescriptors[names.ServiceAccountTokenController]; ok {\n        check, err := StartController(ctx, controllerCtx, serviceAccountTokenControllerDescriptor, unsecuredMux)\n        if err != nil {\n            return err\n        }\n        if check != nil {\n            controllerChecks = append(controllerChecks, check)\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Start all other controllers\n    for _, controllerDesc := range controllerDescriptors {\n        if controllerDesc.RequiresSpecialHandling() {\n            continue\n        }\n        \n        check, err := StartController(ctx, controllerCtx, controllerDesc, unsecuredMux)\n        if err != nil {\n            return err\n        }\n        if check != nil {\n            controllerChecks = append(controllerChecks, check)\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Register all health checks\n    healthzHandler.AddHealthChecker(controllerChecks...)\n    return nil\n}\n```\n\n**Step 5: StartController() - Individual Controller Startup**\n\n```go\nfunc StartController(ctx context.Context, controllerCtx ControllerContext, \n    controllerDescriptor *ControllerDescriptor,\n    unsecuredMux *mux.PathRecorderMux) (healthz.HealthChecker, error) {\n    \n    logger := klog.FromContext(ctx)\n    controllerName := controllerDescriptor.Name()\n\n    // 1. Check feature gates\n    for _, featureGate := range controllerDescriptor.GetRequiredFeatureGates() {\n        if !utilfeature.DefaultFeatureGate.Enabled(featureGate) {\n            return nil, nil\n        }\n    }\n\n    // 2. Skip cloud provider controllers\n    if controllerDescriptor.IsCloudProviderController() {\n        return nil, nil\n    }\n\n    // 3. Check if controller is enabled in config\n    if !controllerCtx.IsControllerEnabled(controllerDescriptor) {\n        return nil, nil\n    }\n\n    // 4. Apply startup jitter\n    time.Sleep(wait.Jitter(controllerCtx.ComponentConfig.Generic.ControllerStartInterval.Duration, ControllerStartJitter))\n\n    // 5. Call the InitFunc - THIS IS WHERE REGISTRATION HAPPENS\n    initFunc := controllerDescriptor.GetInitFunc()\n    ctrl, started, err := initFunc(klog.NewContext(ctx, klog.LoggerWithName(logger, controllerName)), controllerCtx, controllerName)\n    if err != nil {\n        return nil, err\n    }\n    if !started {\n        return nil, nil\n    }\n\n    // 6. Create default health check\n    check := controllerhealthz.NamedPingChecker(controllerName)\n\n    // 7. If controller implements Debuggable, mount debug handler\n    if debuggable, ok := ctrl.(controller.Debuggable); ok && unsecuredMux != nil {\n        if debugHandler := debuggable.DebuggingHandler(); debugHandler != nil {\n            basePath := \"/debug/controllers/\" + controllerName\n            unsecuredMux.UnlistedHandle(basePath, http.StripPrefix(basePath, debugHandler))\n        }\n    }\n\n    // 8. If controller implements HealthCheckable, use custom health check\n    if healthCheckable, ok := ctrl.(controller.HealthCheckable); ok {\n        if realCheck := healthCheckable.HealthChecker(); realCheck != nil {\n            check = controllerhealthz.NamedHealthChecker(controllerName, realCheck)\n        }\n    }\n\n    logger.Info(\"Started controller\", \"controller\", controllerName)\n    return check, nil\n}\n```\n\n### 6. **Key Integration Points**\n\n1. **Controller Discovery**: `NewControllerDescriptors()` centralizes all controller registrations\n2. **Dependency Injection**: `ControllerContext` provides clients, informers, and config\n3. **Feature Gating**: Controllers can be gated behind feature flags\n4. **Conditional Startup**: Controllers can be disabled in configuration\n5. **Health Checks**: Controllers implement `HealthCheckable` interface for `/healthz`\n6. **Debugging**: Controllers implement `Debuggable` interface for `/debug/controllers/{name}`\n7. **Leader Election**: Controllers are started only on the leader node\n8. **Jittered Startup**: Controllers start with random delays to prevent API server overload\n\n### 7. **Controller Client Access Pattern**\n\nControllers get clients via:\n```go\nclientBuilder.ClientOrDie(\"controller-name\")  // Full Kubernetes client\nclientBuilder.DiscoveryClientOrDie(\"controller-name\")  // Discovery client\n```\n\nAnd informers via:\n```go\ncontrollerContext.InformerFactory.Apps().V1().Deployments()  // Typed informer\ncontrollerContext.ObjectOrMetadataInformerFactory.ForResource(gvr)  // Generic informer\n```\n\n### Summary\n\nThe Kubernetes controller registration pattern uses:\n- **ControllerDescriptor** as the registration metadata container\n- **InitFunc** as the factory function that creates and starts controllers\n- **ControllerContext** as the dependency injection container\n- **StartController()** as the orchestration function that handles initialization, feature gates, health checks, and debugging\n- **NewControllerDescriptors()** as the central registry where all controllers self-register\n\nThis design allows ~40+ controllers to be managed in a uniform, pluggable way with proper initialization ordering, feature gating, and lifecycle management.",

:= func(ctx context.Context, controllerDescriptors map[string]*ControllerDescriptor) {\n   228\u2192\t\tcontrollerContext, err := CreateControllerContext(ctx, c, rootClientBuilder, clientBuilder)\n 259\u2192\t// add a uniquifier so that two processes on the same host don't accidentally both become active\n   260\u2192\tid = id + \"_\" + string(uuid.NewUUID())\n   261\u2192\n   262\u2192\t// 363\u2192}\n   364\u2192\n   365\u2192// ControllerContext defines the context object for controller\n   366\u2192type ControllerContext struct {\n   367\u2192\t// ClientBuilder will provide a client for this controller to use\n   368\u2192\tClientBuilder clientbuilder.ControllerClientBuilder\n   369\u2192\n   370\u2192\t// InformerFactory gives access to informers for the controller.\n   371\u2192\tInformerFactory informers.SharedInformerFactory\n   372\u2192\n   373\u2192\t// ObjectOrMetadataInformerFactory gives access to informers for typed resources\n   374\u2192\t// and dynamic resources by their metadata. All generic controllers currently use\n   375\u2192\t// object metadata - if a future controller needs access to the full object this\n   376\u2192\t// would become GenericInformerFactory and take a dynamic client.\n   377\u2192\tObjectOrMetadataInformerFactory informerfactory.InformerFactory\n   378\u2192\n   379\u2192\t// ComponentConfig provides access to init options for a given controller\n   380\u2192\tComponentConfig kubectrlmgrconfig.KubeControllerManagerConfiguration\n   381\u2192\n   382\u2192\t// DeferredDiscoveryRESTMapper is a RESTMapper that will defer\n   383\u2192\t// initialization of the RESTMapper until the first mapping is\n   384\u2192\t// requested.\n   385\u2192\tRESTMapper *restmapper.DeferredDiscoveryRESTMapper\n   386\u2192\n   387\u2192\t// InformersStarted is closed after all of the controllers have been initialized and are running.  After this point it is safe,\n   388\u2192\t// for an individual controller to start the shared informers. Before it is closed, they should not.\n   389\u2192\tInformersStarted chan struct{}\n   390\u2192\n   391\u2192\t// ResyncPeriod generates a duration each time it is invoked; this is so that\n   392\u2192\t// multiple controllers don't get into lock-step and all hammer the apiserver\n   393\u2192\t// with list requests simultaneously.\n   394\u2192\tResyncPeriod func() time.Duration\n   395\u2192\n   396\u2192\t// ControllerManagerMetrics provides a proxy to set controller manager specific metrics.\n   397\u2192\tControllerManagerMetrics *controllersmetrics.ControllerManagerMetrics\n   398\u2192\n   399\u2192\t// GraphBuilder gives an access to dependencyGraphBuilder which keeps tracks of resources in the cluster\n   400\u2192\tGraphBuilder *garbagecollector.GraphBuilder\n   401\u2192}\n   402\u2192\n   403\u2192// IsControllerEnabled checks if the context's controllers enabled or not\n   404\u2192func (c ControllerContext) IsControllerEnabled(controllerDescriptor *ControllerDescriptor) bool {\n   405\u2192\tcontrollersDisabledByDefault := sets.NewString()\n   406\u2192\tif controllerDescriptor.IsDisabledByDefault() {\n   407\u2192\t\tcontrollersDisabledByDefault.Insert(controllerDescriptor.Name())\n   408\u2192\t}\n   409\u2192\treturn genericcontrollermanager.IsControllerEnabled(controllerDescriptor.Name(), controllersDisabledByDefault, c.ComponentConfig.Generic.Controllers)\n   410\u2192}\n   411\u2192\n   412\u2192// InitFunc is used to launch a particular controller. It returns a controller\n   413\u2192// that can optionally implement other interfaces so that the controller manager\n   414\u2192// can support the requested features.\n   415\u2192// The returned controller may be nil, which will be considered an anonymous controller\n   416\u2192// that requests no additional features from the controller manager.\n   417\u2192// Any error returned will cause the controller process to `Fatal`\n   418\u2192// The bool indicates whether the controller was enabled.\n   419\u2192type InitFunc func(ctx context.Context, controllerContext ControllerContext, controllerName string) (controller controller.Interface, enabled bool, err error)\n   420\u2192\n   421\u2192type ControllerDescriptor struct {\n   422\u2192\tname                      string\n   423\u2192\tinitFunc                  InitFunc\n   424\u2192\trequiredFeatureGates      []featuregate.Feature\n   425\u2192\taliases                   []string\n   426\u2192\tisDisabledByDefault       bool\n   427\u2192\tisCloudProviderController bool\n   428\u2192\trequiresSpecialHandling   bool\n   429\u2192}\n   430\u2192\n   431\u2192func (r *ControllerDescriptor) Name() string {\n   432\u2192\treturn r.name\n   433\u2192}\n   434\u2192\n   435\u2192func (r *ControllerDescriptor) GetInitFunc() InitFunc {\n   436\u2192\treturn r.initFunc\n   437\u2192}\n   438\u2192\n   439\u2192func (r *ControllerDescriptor) GetRequiredFeatureGates() []featuregate.Feature {\n   440\u2192\treturn append([]featuregate.Feature(nil), r.requiredFeatureGates...)\n   441\u2192}\n   442\u2192\n   443\u2192// GetAliases returns aliases to ensure backwards compatibility and should never be removed!\n   444\u2192// Only addition of new aliases is allowed, and only when a canonical name is changed (please see CHANGE POLICY of controller names)\n   445\u2192func (r *ControllerDescriptor) GetAliases() []string {\n   446\u2192\treturn append([]string(nil), r.aliases...)\n   447\u2192}\n   448\u2192\n   449\u2192func (r *ControllerDescriptor) IsDisabledByDefault() bool {\n   450\u2192\treturn r.isDisabledByDefault\n   451\u2192}\n   452\u2192\n   453\u2192func (r 460\u2192}\n   461\u2192\n   462\u2192// KnownControllers returns all known controllers's name\n   463\u2192func KnownControllers() []string {\n   464\u2192\treturn sets.StringKeySet(NewControllerDescriptors()).List()\n   465\u2192}\n   466\u2192\n   467\u2192// ControllerAliases returns a mapping of aliases to canonical controller names\n   468\u2192func ControllerAliases() map[string]string {\n   469\u2192\taliases := map[string]string{}\n   470\u2192\tfor name, c := range NewControllerDescriptors() {\n   471\u2192\t\tfor _, alias := range ControllersDisabledByDefault() []string {\n   479\u2192\tvar controllersDisabledByDefault []string\n   480\u2192\n   481\u2192\tfor name, c := range NewControllerDescriptors() {\n   482\u2192\t\tif 487\u2192\tsort.Strings(controllersDisabledByDefault)\n   488\u2192\n   489\u2192\treturn controllersDisabledByDefault\n   490\u2192}\n   491\u2192\n   492\u2192// NewControllerDescriptors is a public map of named controller groups (you can start more than one in an init func)\n   493\u2192// paired to their ControllerDescriptor wrapper object that includes InitFunc.\n   494\u2192// This allows for structured downstream composition and subdivision.\n   495\u2192func NewControllerDescriptors() map[string]*ControllerDescriptor {\n   496\u2192\tcontrollers := map[string]*ControllerDescriptor{}\n   497\u2192\taliases := sets.NewString()\n   498\u2192\n   499\u2192\t// All the controllers must fulfil common constraints, or else we will explode.\n   500\u2192\tregister := func(controllerDesc *ControllerDescriptor) {\n   501\u2192\t\tif controllerDesc == nil {\n   502\u2192\t\t\tpanic(\"received nil controller for a registration\")\n   503\u2192\t\t}\n   504\u2192\t\tname := controllerDesc.Name()\n   505\u2192\t\tif len(name) == 0 {\n   506\u2192\t\t\tpanic(\"received controller without a name for a registration\")\n   507\u2192\t\t}\n   508\u2192\t\tif _, found := controllers[name]; found {\n   509\u2192\t\t\tpanic(fmt.Sprintf(\"controller name %q was registered twice\", name))\n   510\u2192\t\t}\n   511\u2192\t\tif controllerDesc.GetInitFunc() == nil {\n   512\u2192\t\t\tpanic(fmt.Sprintf(\"controller %q does not have an init function\", name))\n   513\u2192\t\t}\n   514\u2192\n   515\u2192\t\tfor _, alias := range controllerDesc.GetAliases() {\n   516\u2192\t\t\tif aliases.Has(alias) {\n   517\u2192\t\t\t\tpanic(fmt.Sprintf(\"controller %q has a duplicate alias %q\", name, alias))\n   518\u2192\t\t\t}\n   519\u2192\t\t\taliases.Insert(alias)\n   520\u2192\t\t}\n   521\u2192\n   522\u2192\t\tcontrollers[name] = controllerDesc\n   523\u2192\t}\n   524\u2192\n   525\u2192\t// First add \"special\" controllers that aren't initialized normally. These controllers cannot be initialized\n   526\u2192\t// in the main controller loop initialization, so we add them here only for the metadata and duplication detection.\n   527\u2192\t// app.ControllerDescriptor#RequiresSpecialHandling should return true for such controllers\n   528\u2192\t// The only known special case is the ServiceAccountTokenController which *must* be started\n   529\u2192\t// first to ensure that the SA tokens for future controllers will exist. Think very carefully before adding new\n   530\u2192\t// special controllers.\n   531\u2192\tregister(newServiceAccountTokenControllerDescriptor(nil))\n   532\u2192\n   533\u2192\tregister(newEndpointsControllerDescriptor())\n   534\u2192\tregister(newEndpointSliceControllerDescriptor())\n   535\u2192\tregister(newEndpointSliceMirroringControllerDescriptor())\n   536\u2192\tregister(newReplicationControllerDescriptor())\n   537\u2192\tregister(newPodGarbageCollectorControllerDescriptor())\n   538\u2192\tregister(newResourceQuotaControllerDescriptor())\n   539\u2192\tregister(newNamespaceControllerDescriptor())\n   540\u2192\tregister(newServiceAccountControllerDescriptor())\n   541\u2192\tregister(newGarbageCollectorControllerDescriptor())\n 548\u2192\tregister(newStatefulSetControllerDescriptor())\n   549\u2192\tregister(newCronJobControllerDescriptor())\n   550\u2192\tregister(newCertificateSigningRequestSigningControllerDescriptor())\n 556\u2192\tregister(newNodeIpamControllerDescriptor())\n   557\u2192\tregister(newNodeLifecycleControllerDescriptor())\n   558\u2192\n   559\u2192\tregister(newServiceLBControllerDescriptor())          // cloud provider controller\n   560\u2192\tregister(newNodeRouteControllerDescriptor())          // cloud provider controller\n   561\u2192\tregister(newCloudNodeLifecycleControllerDescriptor()) // cloud provider controller\n   562\u2192\t// TODO: persistent volume controllers into the IncludeCloudLoops only set as a cloud provider controller.\n   563\u2192\n 566\u2192\tregister(newPersistentVolumeExpanderControllerDescriptor())\n   567\u2192\tregister(newClusterRoleAggregrationControllerDescriptor())\n   568\u2192\tregister(newPersistentVolumeClaimProtectionControllerDescriptor())\n   569\u2192\tregister(newPersistentVolumeProtectionControllerDescriptor())\n controller name\", alias))\n   589\u2192\t\t}\n   590\u2192\t}\n   591\u2192\n   592\u2192\treturn controllers\n   593\u2192}\n   594\u2192\n   595\u2192// CreateControllerContext creates a context struct containing references to resources needed by the\n   596\u2192// controllers such as the cloud provider and clientBuilder. rootClientBuilder is only used for\n   597\u2192// the shared-informers client and token controller.\n   598\u2192func CreateControllerContext(ctx context.Context, s *config.CompletedConfig, rootClientBuilder, clientBuilder clientbuilder.ControllerClientBuilder) (ControllerContext, error) {\n   599\u2192\t// Informer transform to trim ManagedFields for memory efficiency.\n   600\u2192\ttrim := func(obj interface{}) (`cmd/kube-controller-manager/app/controllermanager.go`): The central registration metadata type that contains:\\n- `name`: Canonical controller name (e.g., \\\"deployment\\\")\\n- `initFunc`: A func(ctx context.Context, controllerContext ControllerContext, controllerName string) (controller controller.Interface, enabled bool, err error)\\n```\\n\\n**Interface** (`staging/src/k8s.io/controller-manager/controller/interfaces.go`): The base controller interface that requires:\\n- `Name()`: Returns the controller's canonical name\\n\\nOptional interfaces:\\n- to provide custom health checks for `/healthz` endpoint\\n\\n### Registration and Wiring Process\\n\\n**1. Central Discovery - NewControllerDescriptors()** (`cmd/kube-controller-manager/app/controllermanager.go`): This function creates a map of all ~40 controller descriptors. Each controller registers itself by calling `register(newXControllerDescriptor())`. For example:\\n```\\nregister(newEndpointsControllerDescriptor())\\nregister(newDeploymentControllerDescriptor())\\nregister(newStatefulSetControllerDescriptor())\\n```\\n\\n**2. Individual Controller Descriptor Definition** (`cmd/kube-controller-manager/app/core.go` and similar files): Each controller defines descriptor factory functions like:\\n```\\nfunc newEndpointsControllerDescriptor() *ControllerDescriptor {\\n    return &ControllerDescriptor{\\n        name:     \\\"endpoints-controller\\\",\\n        aliases:  []string{\\\"endpoint\\\"},\\n        initFunc: startEndpointsController,\\n    }\\n}\\n```\\n\\n**3. Manager Orchestration - StartControllers()** (`cmd/kube-controller-manager/app/controllermanager.go`): The controller manager's orchestration function iterates through all descriptors and calls `StartController()` for each one (except those marked `RequiresSpecialHandling()`).\\n\\n**5. Individual Startup - StartController()** (`cmd/kube-controller-manager/app/controllermanager.go`): This function handles:\\n- Checking feature gates required by the controller\\n- Verifying the controller is enabled in configuration\\n- Applying startup jitter to prevent API server overload\\n- Calling the controller's InitFunc (which is the \\\"registration\\\" step)\\n- Mounting debug handlers if the controller implements `Debuggable`\\n- Registering health checks if the controller implements `HealthCheckable`\\n\\n**6. ControllerContext Dependency Injection** (`cmd/kube-controller-manager/app/controllermanager.go`): All controllers receive a `ControllerContext` struct that provides:\\n- `ClientBuilder`: Access to Kubernetes API clients\\n- `InformerFactory`: Access to cached resource watchers\\n- `ComponentConfig`: Controller-specific configuration\\n- `RESTMapper`: API resource discovery\\n- `ResyncPeriod`: Function that returns random sync periods (prevents thundering herd)\\n\\n**7. Actual Controller Implementation** (`pkg/controller/endpoint/endpoints_controller.go`): The concrete controller implements:\\n- Constructor (`NewEndpointController`) that registers event handlers on informers\\n- A `Run()` method that starts worker goroutines processing a work queue\\n- Event handlers that enqueue items when resources change\\n- Worker methods that process items and reconcile state\\n\\n### Reconciliation Loop\\n\\nThe manager's reconcile loop is implemented through:\\n1. **Event-driven queueing**: Informers watch for resource changes and trigger event handlers\\n2. **Work queue**: Items are added to a rate-limited work queue\\n3. **Worker goroutines**: Multiple workers process items from the queue\\n4. **Reconciliation**: Each worker item triggers comparison and reconciliation of desired vs actual state\\n5. **Retries**: Failed items are re-queued with exponential backoff\\n\\n### Leader Election Integration\\n\\nControllers are registered and started within a leader election context. Only the leader node runs the controllers, ensuring single-writer semantics. The `Run()` function in `controllermanager.go` uses `leaderElectAndRun()` to gate controller startup on leader election.\\n\\n### Key Differences from controller-runtime\\n\\nWhile the task mentions controller-runtime patterns (Reconciler interface, SetupWithManager), Kubernetes controllers use its own patterns:\\n- Instead of `SetupWithManager()`, Kubernetes uses the `InitFunc` approach\\n- Instead of a single `Reconcile()` method, Kubernetes controllers implement `Run()` methods with work queues\\n- Instead of manager auto-wiring, Kubernetes manually creates and passes clients/informers via `ControllerContext`\\n\\nThe patterns are semantically equivalent but architecturally different, with Kubernetes' approach being lower-level and more explicit about resource management.\"\n}\n",
